# ThirdParties -1 - -1

1005763=<mailtext><p>I'm sending you all of the information about Yana Rodriguez that is stored in my database.</p><p>Yana Rodriguez appeared at the Eden Initative out of nowhere. As it turned out, it was their leader Seamus Green who personally persuaded Yana to join the organization - just hours after the two had met for the first time. High-ranking members of the organization say that Green was fascinated from the start by the energy Yana radiates. Her brash manner, which disgusts most other people, amused him.<br/><br/>Yana quickly gained Seamus Green's  confidence and goodwill. Her appointment as Representative of the Eden Initative nevertheless caused a great deal of surprise and protest, known as Yana is for her big mouth and her unorthodox methods. Rumors also abounded that she had in truth been hired to get Green out of the way and crush the organization. These rumors are fueled time and again by Yana's behavior. Her murky past and rapid ascent have brought Yana Rodriguez many begrudging skeptics, not only within the Eden Initiative.    </p><p>[GUIDNAME 1005769]</p></mailtext>

Most people have been forced to find other places to live. Sprawling mega Cities could not cope with the influx and social structures, and political institutions simply collapsed. The world was overwhelmed by numerous local conflicts and law and order broke down. The Eden initiative fights for the preservation of the last great nature reserves and for prudent management of the oceans' great riches. Fully committed to the cause of alternative Energy, it promotes the exploration of new green Technologies.</p> <p>The S.A.A.T., Scientific Academy for Advanced Technologies, views these developments with suspicion. This elitist union of the world's most eminent Scientists regards itself as the sole defender of progress. The pioneering achievements of S.A.A.T. will decide the future of the planet, and this is recognized by Global Trust and the Eden Initiative, who are both eager to court the services of S.A.A.T..</p></helperquestmailtext><ul class="helperquestmaillist"></ul></td></tr></table>

# Website Texts -1 - -1

1121639=<b>How does the Ranking system work?</b><br /><br />"Domination points" are awarded for every Domination conflict completed. The number of "Domination points" awarded depends upon the two teams' end scores. Calculations are then made to determine how difficult it was to attain that point score in that match.<br /><br />taken into account are:<br />1) Map type<br />2) Time limit<br />3) Duration<br />4) Team skill levels.<br /><br />The harder the Map was, the shorter the Time limit or Duration and the stronger the opposing team was, the more difficult the match is considered to have been. This calculated level of difficulty now adds an additional bonus to the points scored. These "Conflict points" are then distributed amongst the teams. The winners receive all the points, the losers none.<br /><br />"Conflict points" are only awarded to those players who saw the match through to the end. Anyone who quits before the match ends does not receive any points. 
1121640=Goal

1123284=The World of Techs
1123285=<addonsubline>More than 30 new buildings and vehicles</addonsubline>The needs of the Tech Geniuses are complex and cannot be satisfied easily. Put up many new buildings - most of them underwater - like the Gene Pharming Lab, the Coral Factory or the Electronics Recycler. Discover those and many more new production buildings and master their requirements to perfection to satisfy your Tech Geniuses. 
1123286=Tech Ornaments
1123287=<addonsubline>Make your city more beautiful with the most modern technologies</addonsubline>Techs are mostly interested in efficiency, but even a Genius needs some free time which he likes to spend in a suitable environment. Glass tunnels and holograms will embellish every city. And although the Techs are proud of their technology, they really enjoy a nice walk through a beautiful park.
1123288=Underwater Expansion
1123289=The deep sea is waiting for you
1123290=<addonsubline>New production capacity underwater</addonsubline>Thanks to the technology of the Techs you will be able to expand underwater. Here you can find all the needed resources to satisfy the Techs and keep them happy.
1123291=Underwater trading routes
1123292=<addonsubline>Benefit from the possibilities the underwater world offers</addonsubline>In ANNO 2070: Deep Blue Sea there are underwater trading routes for the first time ever. Use the hidden way of transportation to bring your goods fast and safe from one base to another. It is truly a fascinating spectacle if your submarines dive and surface automatically while they supply your needs.
1123293=Trading Submarines
1123294=<addonsubline>Safe transfer underwater</addonsubline>The new trading submarine of the Sysyphos class offers you completely new trading options. In combination with the underwater trading routes it is now possible to transport goods below water level. This will be an unbeatable advantage if you come into conflict with an opponent. Transport your goods safely and unnoticed through enemy lines.
1123295=New energy
1123296=Geothermal Powerplant
1123297=<addonsubline>The energy source of the future</addonsubline>The Geothermal Powerplant is the strongest powerplant in ANNO 2070 and is the Tech’s answer to mankond’s everlasting need for energy. This monstrous building is able to absorb the nearly limitless energy of the Earth’s core. This is something every ANNO 2070 player needs. But pay attention: Powerful technologies are not easily controlled...
1123298=Energy Transmitter 
1123299=<addonsubline>The answer to all energy problems?</addonsubline>With the help of Energy Transmitters you can transfer electricity between your islands. Thanks to this feature you gain more possibilities to plan your cities. Change the appearance of your cities or even complete islands by relocating your energy production. This is a huge step towards solving all your energy problems.
1123300=Tsunami
1123301=<addonsubline>A massive threat for your cities</addonsubline>Advantages are great - but at what price? This is especially true for the Geothermal Powerplant. On the one hand, it provides you with nearly endless energy. On the other hand, a malfunction can become a massive threat for the surrounding islands. Although, a Tsunami may look impressive, it is recommended to have some items on stock to avoid the catastrophe.

# Tooltip 1810700 - 1810799



# Starttips 1815200 - 1816199
#-----------------------------

1815200=Left-click to select your Ship and right-click on any point on the map to sail it there.
1815201=Use your Ships to explore the game world and discover new Islands and other parties!
1815202=When colonizing new Islands, remember that you can only build Warehouses on flat stretches of beach.
1815203=Hold down the middle mouse button and move the mouse to rotate the game world at will.
1815204=The game settings enable you to display all the audio commentaries as text. Alternatively, you can use the key combination "[BINDING / game / togglesubtitles]."
1815205=Use the mouse wheel to change the camera height.
1815206=Connect Buildings by Roads so that your Population's Needs can be satisfied and Goods can be collected.
1815207=All Production facilities require Road connections to allow you to deliver and collect Goods.
1815208=Plants, Ships and Military units all incur ongoing Maintenance costs. You can save a portion of those costs by shutting down Plants.
1815209=Move your mouse over the Balance and Population displays to obtain a detailed breakdown of those values​​.
1815210=A positive Balance increases your wealth every second, while a negative Balance reduces it, so avoid long periods in the red!
1815211=Most Buildings consume Energy. If there is not enough Energy available on the Island they will not operate at full strength.
1815212=In the event of an Energy shortage, you should build new Power plants or shut down Plants.
1815213=The data log is a collection of all the help messages E.V.E. has compiled for you to date.
1815214=Abandoned Workers' Residences will be repaired automatically as soon as the Workers' Needs will again be satisfied and new Inhabitants will move in.
1815215=The info bar provides information not only about your inventories and your Capital, but also about Island Fertilities and Raw material deposits.
1815216=Left-click the arrow next to an Island's Fertility display to show its Raw material deposits.
1815217=You can automatically create Production facilities for Plants using the large "Build Production automatically" button in the Building menu.
1815218=The better the Ecobalance on your Island, the more your Crops will flourish and the more satisfied your Inhabitants will be.
1815219=There are special Buildings which improve your Ecobalance. You can use them to offset the Pollution produced by your Production plants.
1815220=Particularly advanced Eco Technology can greatly improve an Island's Ecobalance. You then will profit from Production bonuses and increased Satisfaction levels.
1815221=Tycoon Buildings can only repair an Island's Ecobalance, not improve it. You will need Eco Technology to achieve a positive Ecobalance.
1815222=A very low Ecobalance can trigger devastating environmental disasters that will cause far more damage to your Production than normal.
1815223=Hold down the right mouse button and move the mouse to scroll the screen in any direction.
1815224=Hold down the "+" key to increase the game speed.
1815225=Mines are built directly over Raw material deposits. Remember to have the mined Raw material collected or processed on site.
1815226=Left-click to select a Residence to obtain detailed information about the different Needs for a specific Level of civilization.
1815227=Left-clicking the Tax load in the Residence allows you to set the Tax rate at the maximum value for that Level of civilization.
1815228=When you reach a new Level of civilization, you can immediately access new Buildings. Additional Buildings will be added as your City grows and the Population develops new Needs.
1815229=If you have the required Building materials on board, you can build Warehouses using any of your Ships.
1815230=In ANNO 2070, the Inhabitants at a particular Level of civilization cannot all advance to next level up at the same time. Build more housing for Workers to obtain more Ascension rights.
1815231=Warehouses and Market buildings provide an overview of all the Goods that are available on an Island. The Stocks are sorted by Level of civilization.
1815232=You can use the Residence menu to block and release individual Goods for each Level of civilization.
1815233=Help your neighbors by carrying out Quests for them; you can generally earn valuable rewards for completing them.
1815234=The Diplomacy menu allows you to view your current influence with your neighbors. If you have enough influence, you can demand every effective assistance from them.
1815235=Your neighbors will closely monitor for whom you complete Quests or against whom you wage War; this may increase or reduce your influence with them.
1815236=Successfully completing Quests often brings rewards in the form of Goods, Credits, Licenses or Items.
1815237=Use your Licenses to purchase Items from your neighbors that have special effects.
1815238=The Diplomacy menu allows you to trade your Credits for Licenses with some of your Neighbors.
1815239=High Trade volumes can significantly increase your influence with certain parties.
1815240=Increase your influence with your neighbors by successfully completing Quests.
1815241=To attack enemy Ships, select one of your own Ships and then right-click the enemy.
1815242=Use the Goods transfer button to transfer Goods between Ships and Warehouses.
1815243=In multi-part Production chains, the ratio of one Production plant to another is not necessarily 1:1. Check the Productivity of individual Plants from time to time.
1815244=Is your bank account empty? Tax income, Trade or completing Quests will soon replenish your coffers!
1815245=Some of your neighbors charge significantly more money for their Goods than others, so check the price before making a Trade.
1815246=You can make Peace with Hector like you can with all the other parties. However, he will regularly charge you a high price to maintain that situation.
1815247=Hector also offer Items for sale which honest people would probably call illegal Goods...
1815248=Trade routes to your neighbors allow you to sell surpluses direct to their Warehouses at good prices.
1815249=Buy Intermediate goods from one of your neighbors to save space, Energy and environmental costs for your own Production plants.
1815250=Align Buildings individually before construction using the "[BINDING /game/Rotate(-1)]" or "[BINDING /game/Rotate(1)]" buttons.
1815251=To quick save your game, press the "[BINDING /quicksave]" key, to quick load the "[BINDING /quickload]" key.
1815252=Use Seeds to add any chosen Fertility to an Island. Seeds are available for all Fertilities and can be purchased from many of your neighbors.
1815253=Check your neighbors' selection of Items before colonizing an Island. Maybe they are selling Seeds for a Fertility you are lacking on your Island.
1815254=Start an Escort by selecting one of your Ships and right-clicking on one of your own Ships or an allied one.
1815255=You can rename your Ships by clicking on the name in the Ship menu. Press Enter to confirm your entry.
1815256=You can rename your Warehouses by clicking the name in the Warehouse menu. Press Enter to confirm your entry.
1815257=Expanding Warehouses and Goods depots increases the number of available Goods transport units.
1815258=At their highest level of expansion, Goods depots even allow Goods to be picked up without Road connections via Air drones.
1815259=You can block the awarding of Ascension rights using the button in the Town center Building menu. This prevents your Population from going to the Warehouse and helping themselves to the Goods they require to upgrade.
1815260=Nuclear power plants produce a large amount of Energy very cheaply. The longer a Nuclear power plant is active however, the greater the risk of a nuclear accident.
1815261=You can set the exact rate of Tax by holding down the Shift key and adjusting the Tax load.
1815262=The Construction of Harbor depots in your Harbors considerably increases the quantity of Goods you are able to store on an Island.
1815263=If you block the Ascension rights using the Town center, you can decide which individual Building can upgrade to the next Level of civilization, and when.
1815264=Once Metropolis status is achieved, Eco and Tycoon Executives will start demanding new Goods. There will be no Population increase at this Level of civilization in your City until you provide those Goods.
1815265=Adjust your Ship's routes individually in the Trade route overview by dragging and dropping the waypoints to move them.
1815266=You can always sell your surplus Goods at your neighbors' headquarters.
1815267=You can build Clearance terminals to allow several Ships to Trade and unload their Cargo in your Harbor simultaneously.
1815268=Any Buildings and buttons you drag and drop into the middle of the screen will then be available in the Right-click menu.
1815269=Any Buildings and buttons you drag and drop onto the bottom of the screen will then be available in the Action bar.
1815270=You can use drag and drop to transfer the contents of entire Cargo holds when moving Goods between Ships and Warehouses.
1815271=To save operating costs, you can temporarily shut down Plants using the button in the Building menu.
1815272=The "[BINDING /game/wm/toggleships(0)]" key allows you to toggle back and forth between the Ships in your Fleet.
1815273=With the "[BINDING /game/wm/togglewarehouses(0)]" key allows you to toggle between your Warehouses.
1815274=You can use the Message filter in the News bar on the left to select which messages to display in that bar.
1815276=You can use the filter at the top left of the Strategic map to display or hide additional information.
1815277=You can turn the data log on or off in the game settings in the main menu and therefore decide whether you want to receive tips from E.V.E. during gameplay.
1815278=You can reset the message log at any time via the main menu to obtain more gameplay hints from E.V.E..
1815279=You can visit some of your neighbors to buy new Ships for your Fleet or sell off old Ships.
1815280=Create screenshots using the "[BINDING KD_HARDCOPY]" key. These are stored in the [SCREENSHOT_PATH] folder.
1815281=In the Town center menu you will find detailed information on Tax income and the Energy and Eco costs of your Buildings on that Island.
1815282=You can use the Town center menu to allow Inhabitants to upgrade individually without having to select every single Residence. Use the arrow next to each Population group.
1815283=You can build several Residences simultaneously by holding down the left mouse button and dragging the mouse while positioning a Residence.
1815284=You can right-click on a Goods item in a Warehouse or Goods depot to determine how many tons of that Item must remain on the Island at all times.
1815285=All Raw material deposits on Islands are limited. However, some Research projects and Items enable depleted Resources to be replenished.
1815286=You can drag any Goods item from the Warehouse and Market building menus into the info bar to monitor your Supplies. You can move the Goods icons from the info bar to remove them again.
1815287=You can specify different game objectives during the game setup if you want to set yourself extra challenges in a continuous game.
1815288=Drag Goods from the Warehouse into the info bar at the top of the screen to monitor your Stock levels.
1815289=When building a Warehouse, hold down the Shift key to prevent surplus Goods from being unloaded from the Ship and into the Warehouse.
1815290=If you want to halt Production in all the Plants of a single type simultaneously on an Island, hold down the Shift key when you click the Shutdown button.
1815291=The Command console contains additional useful information about your current game.
1815292=The function database in the Command console enables you to add actions to your Right-click menu which would otherwise only available via keyboard shortcut.
1815293=You can find a detailed list of your current Military units and Warehouses in the "Fleet and Building" tab in the Command console.
1815294=You can find a detailed breakdown of your current game under Mission rankings in the Command console.
1815295=You can find your current game settings and the number of the random maps you are playing in the Command console under "Game Settings".
1815296=Left-click the "Central menu" button or pressing the Esc key to use many of the main menu features without quitting your current game.
1815297=If you activate the postcard view using "[BINDING /game/togglepostcardview]" while a Ship is selected, you can follow it on its journey.
1815298=Use the "[BINDING /game/togglepostcardview]" key to activate the postcard view and move freely through your Settlement.
1815299=If you store valuable Items or Goods in your Ark, they will also be available when you start a new game.
1815300=When you create a new game you can deactivate Ark storage. When you do this, the Ark will be empty when the game starts and no Items or Goods can be stored there for later games.
1815301=Your player profile contains a list of all the titles and medals you can earn in ANNO 2070. However, in some cases you must find out for yourself what you have to do to get them…
1815302=You can enhance your Ark by socketing special Items in it. The bonuses these Items offer will then be available in all other games as well.
1815303=Any daily or World Event assignments you complete will earn you career points with the factions. Your current career status is shown in your player profile.
1815304=Senate elections let you have a say in which advantages and disadvantages will apply to all continuous games and single missions. All ANNO 2070 players are eligible to vote in Senate elections.
1815305=All the ANNO 2070 players can elect the World Council. Depending on which faction the current President belongs to, you can trigger different special actions on your Ark.
1815306=If you hold down the Shift key while transferring Goods between a Ship and a Warehouse, a window will appear where you can set the exact amount to be transferred.
1815307=If you want to quickly weaken your opponent's Naval fleet, activate a detonator on one of your Ships and sail it right into the enemy formation.
1815308=As long as a protection symbol Item is activated on your Ship it cannot be attacked by any other Ship.
1815309=Use a Boarding party to board enemy Ships and add them to your Fleet.
1815310=Socketing and activating a camouflage Item in one of your Ships makes it invisible to your enemies for a limited period of time.
1815311=If you activate an ID Anonymizer on your Ship you can attack another player's Ships regardless of your agreement status.
1815312=If you have a Tycoon, Eco or Tech Residence selected, you can use the "[BINDING /game/ChangeVariation]" key to toggle through the different Building variations. The "[BINDING /game/Rotate(-1)]" and "[BINDING /game/Rotate(-1)]" keys allow you to rotate the Residences in 90° steps.
1815313=Hold the Ctrl key down when building Harbor buildings to automatically build a Harbor wall on the next stretch of Coast or at nearest Harbor building. Alternatively, you can use pipette mode to copy a section of existing Harbor wall.
1815314=All Goods depots that are connected to the Warehouse via the Road network receive an additional Transport unit as a bonus.
1815315=Don't like the name of a City or Ship? You can change it at any time by clicking on the name.
1815316=In multiplayer games you can use Alt + Left-click on the minimap to generate a ping on the map to indicate a specific position to the other players.
